            # But we need to check: the new __MLDATA vmaddr might differ from old __LINKEDIT vmaddr
            # if we placed it at a different vmaddr
            # Since we set ml_vmaddr = old li_vmaddr, the offset is the same!
            # But wait, we need to recalculate because the method lists are at different positions
            # in the new segment vs the old __LINKEDIT
            
            # old_vmaddr of method list data was in __LINKEDIT: li_vmaddr + (fileoff - li_fileoff)
            # new_vmaddr of method list data is in __MLDATA: ml_vmaddr + offset_in_ml_data
            # The ml_old_to_new map has the vmaddr conversion
            
            # For individual rebase entries (pointer fields within method lists),
            # we need to know which method list they belong to and what the new offset is
            
            # The rebase entry's vmaddr in old __LINKEDIT = li_vmaddr + off
            # The method list starts at old_vmaddr, new_vmaddr = ml_old_to_new[old_vmaddr]
            # The entry's offset within the method list = vmaddr - old_vmaddr

            # The entry's new offset in segment 4 = new_vmaddr + (vmaddr - old_vmaddr) - ml_vmaddr
            
            for m in method_lists_in_linkedit:

                    new_ml_vmaddr = ml_old_to_new[m['old_vmaddr']]
                    offset_in_ml = vmaddr - m['old_vmaddr']
                    new_off_in_seg = (new_ml_vmaddr - ml_vmaddr) + offset_in_ml
                    ml_rebases.append((typ, 4, new_off_in_seg))
                    break
            else:
                # Shouldn't happen
                non_ml_rebases.append((typ, seg, off))
        else:
            non_ml_rebases.append((typ, seg, off))
    else:
        non_ml_rebases.append((typ, seg, off))

orig_linkedit_data = data[0x1d0000:0x216228]  # Original __LINKEDIT content

            struct.pack_into('<Q', final, off2+24, new_li_vmaddr_final)  # vmaddr

            struct.pack_into('<Q', final, off2+40, new_li_fileoff)  # fileoff
            struct.pack_into('<Q', final, off2+48, new_li_filesize)  # filesize
            print(f"\nUpdated __LINKEDIT at cmd offset {off2}")
    elif cmd == 0x80000022:  # LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY
        struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+8, final_rebase_off)
        struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+12, len(new_rebase))
        struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+16, final_bind_off)
        struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+20, len(cur_bind))
        struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+40, new_export_off)
        struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+44, export_size)
        print(f"Updated LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY at cmd offset {off2}")
    elif cmd == 0x02:  # LC_SYMTAB
        # symoff and stroff need adjusting if they were in __LINKEDIT
        old_symoff = struct.unpack_from('<I', final, off2+8)[0]
        old_stroff = struct.unpack_from('<I', final, off2+16)[0]
        if old_symoff >= 0x1d0000:
            new_symoff = new_li_fileoff + (old_symoff - 0x1d0000)
            struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+8, new_symoff)
        if old_stroff >= 0x1d0000:
            new_stroff = new_li_fileoff + (old_stroff - 0x1d0000)
            struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+16, new_stroff)
            print(f"Updated LC_SYMTAB: symoff 0x{old_symoff:x}->0x{new_symoff:x} stroff 0x{old_stroff:x}->0x{new_stroff:x}")
    elif cmd == 0x0b:  # LC_DYSYMTAB
        # Update indirect sym table offset if needed
        old_indoff = struct.unpack_from('<I', final, off2+8*8)[0]  # Actually at specific offset
        # LC_DYSYMTAB has many fields, but indirectsymoff is already 0, so skip
        pass
    elif cmd == 0x26:  # LC_FUNCTION_STARTS
        old_off = struct.unpack_from('<I', final, off2+8)[0]
        if old_off >= 0x1d0000:
            new_off = new_li_fileoff + (old_off - 0x1d0000)
            struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+8, new_off)
            print(f"Updated LC_FUNCTION_STARTS: 0x{old_off:x}->0x{new_off:x}")
    elif cmd == 0x1d:  # LC_CODE_SIGNATURE
        old_off = struct.unpack_from('<I', final, off2+8)[0]
        if old_off >= 0x1d0000:
            new_off = new_li_fileoff + (old_off - 0x1d0000)
            struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+8, new_off)
            print(f"Updated LC_CODE_SIGNATURE: 0x{old_off:x}->0x{new_off:x}")
    elif cmd == 0x2a:  # LC_DATA_IN_CODE
        old_off = struct.unpack_from('<I', final, off2+8)[0]
        if old_off >= 0x1d0000:
            new_off = new_li_fileoff + (old_off - 0x1d0000)
            struct.pack_into('<I', final, off2+8, new_off)
            print(f"Updated LC_DATA_IN_CODE: 0x{old_off:x}->0x{new_off:x}")
    off2 += cmdsize

# Also need to update method list pointers to use new vmaddr
for m in method_lists_in_linkedit:
    new_vm = ml_old_to_new[m['old_vmaddr']]
    # The new vmaddr was calculated based on ml_vmaddr = li_vmaddr = 0x1d4000
    # which matches our ml_seg_vmaddr, so the pointers should be correct
    struct.pack_into('<Q', final, m['ro_ptr_off'], new_vm)

with open('libFosterPlatform.dylib', 'wb') as f:
    f.write(final)
print(f"\nWrote {len(final)} bytes")

Rebuild from scratch with correct layout
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import struct

# Start completely fresh from the patched x64 binary
# Apply ALL changes at once to avoid cascading offset bugs

with open('libFosterPlatform_x64.dylib','rb') as f:
    data = bytearray(f.read())

print(f"Original file: {len(data)} bytes")

# ===== STEP 1: Parse original chained fixups binary =====
off = 32
ncmds_orig = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, 16)[0]
sizeofcmds_orig = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, 20)[0]
segs = []
exports_off = exports_size = fixups_off = fixups_size = 0
to_remove = []  # (offset, size)

lc_off = 32
for i in range(ncmds_orig):
    cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack_from('<II', data, lc_off)
    if cmd == 0x19:
        segname = data[lc_off+8:lc_off+24].split(b'\x00')[0].decode()
        vmaddr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, lc_off+24)[0]
        segs.append({'name': segname, 'vmaddr': vmaddr, 
                     'vmsize': struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, lc_off+32)[0],
                     'fileoff': struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, lc_off+40)[0],
                     'filesize': struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, lc_off+48)[0],
                     'cmd_off': lc_off})
    elif cmd == 0x80000033:  # LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE
        exports_off = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, lc_off+8)[0]
        exports_size = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, lc_off+12)[0]
        to_remove.append((lc_off, cmdsize))
    elif cmd == 0x80000034:  # LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS
        fixups_off = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, lc_off+8)[0]
        fixups_size = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, lc_off+12)[0]
        to_remove.append((lc_off, cmdsize))
    elif cmd == 0x32:  # LC_BUILD_VERSION
        to_remove.append((lc_off, cmdsize))
    lc_off += cmdsize

print(f"Segments: {[s['name'] for s in segs]}")
print(f"Exports: off=0x{exports_off:x} size={exports_size}")
print(f"Fixups: off=0x{fixups_off:x} size={fixups_size}")

# ===== STEP 2: Parse chained fixups and collect rebase/bind data =====
cfh = struct.unpack_from('<7I', data, fixups_off)
starts_base = fixups_off + cfh[1]
imports_base = fixups_off + cfh[2]
symbols_base = fixups_off + cfh[3]
imports_count = cfh[4]

seg_count = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, starts_base)[0]

def encode_uleb(v):
    r = bytearray()
    while True:
        b = v & 0x7F; v >>= 7
        if v: b |= 0x80
        r.append(b)
        if not v: break
    return bytes(r)

rebase_entries = []  # (seg_idx, off_in_seg, target_vmaddr)
bind_entries = []    # (seg_idx, off_in_seg, lib_ordinal, weak, symbol_name, addend)

for si in range(min(seg_count, len(segs))):
    sio = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, starts_base + 4 + si * 4)[0]
    if sio == 0: continue
    
    ss_base = starts_base + sio
    page_size = struct.unpack_from('<H', data, ss_base + 4)[0]
    ptr_format = struct.unpack_from('<H', data, ss_base + 6)[0]
    page_count = struct.unpack_from('<H', data, ss_base + 20)[0]
    
    for pg in range(page_count):
        ps = struct.unpack_from('<H', data, ss_base + 22 + pg * 2)[0]
        if ps == 0xFFFF: continue
        
        off_in_seg = pg * page_size + ps
        while True:
            file_pos = segs[si]['fileoff'] + off_in_seg
            raw = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, file_pos)[0]
            is_bind = (raw >> 63) & 1
            next_v = ((raw >> 51) & 0xFFF) * 4
            
            if is_bind:
                ordinal = raw & 0xFFFFFF
                addend = (raw >> 24) & 0xFF
                if addend > 127: addend -= 256
                
                bits = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, imports_base + ordinal * 4)[0]
                lib_ord = bits & 0xFF
                if lib_ord > 127: lib_ord -= 256
                weak = (bits >> 8) & 1
                name_off = bits >> 9
                sym = data[symbols_base + name_off:].split(b'\x00')[0].decode()
                
                bind_entries.append((si, off_in_seg, lib_ord, weak, sym, addend))
                # Clear pointer for bind
                struct.pack_into('<Q', data, file_pos, 0)
            else:
                target = raw & 0xFFFFFFFFF  # 36 bits for PTR_64_OFFSET
                high8 = (raw >> 36) & 0xFF
                actual_target = target | (high8 << 56)
                
                rebase_entries.append((si, off_in_seg))
                # Set pointer to target vmaddr
                struct.pack_into('<Q', data, file_pos, actual_target)
            
            if next_v == 0: break
            off_in_seg += next_v

print(f"Fixups: {len(rebase_entries)} rebases, {len(bind_entries)} binds")

# ===== STEP 3: Patch section types =====
for si_idx, seg in enumerate(segs):
    nsects = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, seg['cmd_off']+64)[0]
    for j in range(nsects):
        soff = seg['cmd_off'] + 72 + j * 80
        sectname = data[soff:soff+16].split(b'\x00')[0].decode()
        flags_off = soff + 64
        flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, flags_off)[0]
        stype = flags & 0xFF
        
        if sectname == '__got' and stype == 6:  # S_NON_LAZY_SYMBOL_POINTERS
            struct.pack_into('<I', data, flags_off, flags & ~0xFF)
            struct.pack_into('<I', data, soff+68, 0)  # clear reserved1
            print(f"Patched __got: S_REGULAR")
        elif sectname == '__stubs' and stype == 8:  # S_SYMBOL_STUBS
            struct.pack_into('<I', data, flags_off, flags & ~0xFF)
            struct.pack_into('<I', data, soff+68, 0)
            print(f"Patched __stubs: S_REGULAR")

# ===== STEP 4: Convert relative method lists to absolute =====
methlist_off = 0x182820
methlist_end = methlist_off + 0xd04

# Find all class_ro_t method list references
classlist_off = 0x1c1a98
classlist_size = 0x88
method_list_refs = []  # (ro_ptr_off_for_methods, old_methods_addr)

for i in range(classlist_size // 8):
    class_ptr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, classlist_off + i * 8)[0]
    if not (0 < class_ptr < len(data)): continue
    for label in ['class', 'meta']:
        cur = class_ptr
        if label == 'meta':
            cur = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, class_ptr)[0]
            if not (0 < cur < len(data)): break
        ro = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cur + 32)[0]
        if not (0 < ro < len(data)): continue
        ml = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, ro + 32)[0]
        if not (methlist_off <= ml < methlist_end): continue
        flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml)[0]
        if flags & 0x80000000:
            method_list_refs.append((ro + 32, ml))

# Also categories
catlist_off = 0x1c1b20
for i in range(0x8 // 8):
    cat = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, catlist_off + i * 8)[0]
    if not (0 < cat < len(data)): continue
    for moff in [16, 24]:
        ml = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cat + moff)[0]
        if not (methlist_off <= ml < methlist_end): continue
        flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml)[0]
        if flags & 0x80000000:
            method_list_refs.append((cat + moff, ml))

print(f"Found {len(method_list_refs)} relative method list references")

# Build absolute method lists
# Place them at the end of the file in a new writable segment
# Virtual address: right after __DATA's vmaddr+vmsize = 0x1c4000+0x10000 = 0x1d4000
# That's where __LINKEDIT currently is. We'll shift __LINKEDIT.

new_ml_vmaddr = segs[3]['vmaddr']  # 0x1d4000 (old __LINKEDIT vmaddr)
new_ml_data = bytearray()
ml_ptr_fixups = {}  # old_ml_addr -> new_vmaddr
ml_rebase_entries = []  # (new_seg_idx, off_in_seg) for method list pointers

for ptr_off, old_ml in method_list_refs:
    if old_ml in ml_ptr_fixups:
        # Already converted
        continue
    
    flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, old_ml)[0]
    count = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, old_ml + 4)[0]
    new_flags = flags & ~0x80000000
    
    # Align to 8
    while len(new_ml_data) % 8 != 0:
        new_ml_data.append(0)
    
    new_vmaddr = new_ml_vmaddr + len(new_ml_data)
    ml_ptr_fixups[old_ml] = new_vmaddr
    
    ml_header = struct.pack('<II', new_flags, count)
    new_ml_data.extend(ml_header)
    
    for j in range(count):
        ebase = old_ml + 8 + j * 12
        sel_rel = struct.unpack_from('<i', data, ebase)[0]
        types_rel = struct.unpack_from('<i', data, ebase + 4)[0]
        imp_rel = struct.unpack_from('<i', data, ebase + 8)[0]
        
        sel_ref_addr = ebase + sel_rel
        types_addr = ebase + 4 + types_rel
        imp_addr = ebase + 8 + imp_rel
        
        name_ptr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, sel_ref_addr)[0] if 0 < sel_ref_addr < len(data)-8 else 0
        
        entry_offset_in_seg = len(new_ml_data) + (new_vmaddr - new_ml_vmaddr - len(new_ml_data) + len(new_ml_data))
        # Actually, the entry will be at new_vmaddr + 8 + j * 24
        # But we're building new_ml_data sequentially, so:
        cur_offset_in_seg = len(new_ml_data)
        
        new_ml_data.extend(struct.pack('<QQQ', name_ptr, types_addr, imp_addr))
        
        # Each of these 3 pointers needs a rebase entry
        base_off = new_vmaddr + 8 + j * 24 - new_ml_vmaddr
        ml_rebase_entries.append((base_off,))      # name
        ml_rebase_entries.append((base_off + 8,))   # types
        ml_rebase_entries.append((base_off + 16,))   # imp

print(f"Built {len(ml_ptr_fixups)} absolute method lists, {len(ml_rebase_entries)} rebase entries")

# ===== STEP 5: Build file layout =====
# File layout:
# [0, 0x1d0000) = original __TEXT, __DATA_CONST, __DATA (patched)
# [0x1d0000, 0x1d0000+ml_pad) = __MLDATA segment (method lists)
# [0x1d0000+ml_pad, ...) = __LINKEDIT (original + rebase + bind)

ml_padded = (len(new_ml_data) + 0xFFF) & ~0xFFF  # Page-aligned
ml_seg_vmsize = ml_padded
ml_seg_filesize = len(new_ml_data)
ml_seg_fileoff = 0x1d0000

# Shift __LINKEDIT
new_li_fileoff = 0x1d0000 + ml_padded
new_li_vmaddr = new_ml_vmaddr + ml_seg_vmsize  # 0x1d4000 + vmsize

# Copy original __LINKEDIT data
orig_li_fileoff = segs[3]['fileoff']  # 0x1d0000
orig_li_filesize = segs[3]['filesize']  # 0x46228
orig_li_data = bytes(data[orig_li_fileoff:orig_li_fileoff + orig_li_filesize])
li_shift = new_li_fileoff - orig_li_fileoff

# Build output file
output = bytearray(data[:0x1d0000])  # __TEXT, __DATA_CONST, __DATA

# Add __MLDATA
output.extend(new_ml_data)
output.extend(b'\x00' * (ml_padded - len(new_ml_data)))  # pad to page

# Add __LINKEDIT original data
output.extend(orig_li_data)

# Pad for alignment
while len(output) % 8 != 0:
    output.append(0)

# ===== STEP 6: Generate rebase + bind opcodes =====
# New segment layout: 0=TEXT, 1=DATA_CONST, 2=DATA, 3=LINKEDIT, 4=MLDATA
# But we need to be careful with ordering. Let me keep the load command order as:
# TEXT, DATA_CONST, DATA, MLDATA, LINKEDIT
# So segment indices: 0=TEXT, 1=DATA_CONST, 2=DATA, 3=MLDATA, 4=LINKEDIT
# This means __LINKEDIT moves from index 3 to index 4

# Generate rebase opcodes
rebase_buf = bytearray()
rebase_buf.append(0x11)  # SET_TYPE_IMM | POINTER

# Original rebases (segments 1 and 2 only)
for seg, off in sorted(rebase_entries):
    rebase_buf.append(0x20 | seg)
    rebase_buf.extend(encode_uleb(off))
    rebase_buf.append(0x51)  # DO_REBASE_IMM_TIMES | 1

# Method list rebases (segment 3 = __MLDATA)
for (off,) in sorted(ml_rebase_entries):
    rebase_buf.append(0x20 | 3)  # __MLDATA is segment 3
    rebase_buf.extend(encode_uleb(off))
    rebase_buf.append(0x51)

rebase_buf.append(0x00)  # DONE

rebase_foff = len(output)
output.extend(rebase_buf)
while len(output) % 8 != 0:
    output.append(0)

# Generate bind opcodes
bind_buf = bytearray()
bind_buf.append(0x51)  # SET_TYPE_IMM | POINTER

for seg, off, lib_ord, weak, sym, addend in bind_entries:
    if 0 <= lib_ord < 16:
        bind_buf.append(0x10 | lib_ord)
    elif lib_ord < 0:
        # Special ordinals: -1=main, -2=flat, -3=weak
        bind_buf.append(0x30 | (lib_ord & 0x0F))
    else:
        bind_buf.append(0x20)
        bind_buf.extend(encode_uleb(lib_ord))
    
    flags = 0x01 if weak else 0x00
    bind_buf.append(0x40 | flags)
    bind_buf.extend(sym.encode() + b'\x00')
    
    if addend != 0:
        bind_buf.append(0x60)  # SET_ADDEND_SLEB
        # SLEB128 encoding
        v = addend
        while True:
            b = v & 0x7F; v >>= 7
            if (v == 0 and (b & 0x40) == 0) or (v == -1 and (b & 0x40)):
                bind_buf.append(b)
                break
            bind_buf.append(b | 0x80)
    
    bind_buf.append(0x70 | seg)
    bind_buf.extend(encode_uleb(off))
    bind_buf.append(0x90)  # DO_BIND

bind_buf.append(0x00)  # DONE

bind_foff = len(output)
output.extend(bind_buf)

print(f"Rebase: off=0x{rebase_foff:x} size={len(rebase_buf)}")
print(f"Bind: off=0x{bind_foff:x} size={len(bind_buf)}")
print(f"Exports: off=0x{exports_off + li_shift:x} size={exports_size}")

# ===== STEP 7: Remove old load commands and add new ones =====
# Remove: LC_DYLD_EXPORTS_TRIE, LC_DYLD_CHAINED_FIXUPS, LC_BUILD_VERSION
# Add: LC_SEGMENT_64 (__MLDATA), LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY

# Sort to_remove by offset descending
to_remove.sort(key=lambda x: x[0], reverse=True)
lcmds_end = 32 + sizeofcmds_orig
ncmds = ncmds_orig

for pos, sz in to_remove:
    tail = lcmds_end - (pos + sz)
    output[pos:pos+tail] = output[pos+sz:pos+sz+tail]
    output[pos+tail:lcmds_end] = b'\x00' * sz  # Zero out freed space
    lcmds_end -= sz
    ncmds -= 1

sizeofcmds_new = lcmds_end - 32
print(f"After removing {len(to_remove)} cmds: ncmds={ncmds} sizeofcmds={sizeofcmds_new}")

# Add LC_SEGMENT_64 for __MLDATA (before __LINKEDIT)
# First find __LINKEDIT's load command position
li_cmd_off = None
off2 = 32
for i in range(ncmds):
    cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack_from('<II', output, off2)
    if cmd == 0x19:
        segname = output[off2+8:off2+24].split(b'\x00')[0].decode()
        if segname == '__LINKEDIT':
            li_cmd_off = off2
            break
    off2 += cmdsize

# Write __MLDATA segment command at current lcmds_end
ml_cmd_off = lcmds_end
ml_cmd = bytearray(72)
struct.pack_into('<II', ml_cmd, 0, 0x19, 72)  # LC_SEGMENT_64, cmdsize=72
ml_cmd[8:8+8] = b'__MLDATA'
struct.pack_into('<QQQQ', ml_cmd, 24, new_ml_vmaddr, ml_seg_vmsize, ml_seg_fileoff, ml_seg_filesize)
struct.pack_into('<IIII', ml_cmd, 56, 7, 3, 0, 0)  # maxprot=rwx, initprot=rw, nsects=0, flags=0
output[ml_cmd_off:ml_cmd_off+72] = ml_cmd
lcmds_end += 72
ncmds += 1

# Add LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY
di_cmd_off = lcmds_end
di_cmd = bytearray(48)
struct.pack_into('<II', di_cmd, 0, 0x80000022, 48)
struct.pack_into('<II', di_cmd, 8, rebase_foff, len(rebase_buf))
struct.pack_into('<II', di_cmd, 16, bind_foff, len(bind_buf))
struct.pack_into('<II', di_cmd, 24, 0, 0)  # weak
struct.pack_into('<II', di_cmd, 32, 0, 0)  # lazy
struct.pack_into('<II', di_cmd, 40, exports_off + li_shift, exports_size)
output[di_cmd_off:di_cmd_off+48] = di_cmd
lcmds_end += 48
ncmds += 1

sizeofcmds_new = lcmds_end - 32

# Update header
struct.pack_into('<I', output, 16, ncmds)
struct.pack_into('<I', output, 20, sizeofcmds_new)
print(f"Final: ncmds={ncmds} sizeofcmds={sizeofcmds_new}")

# Update __LINKEDIT segment in the load commands
off2 = 32
for i in range(ncmds):
    cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack_from('<II', output, off2)
    if cmd == 0x19:
        segname = output[off2+8:off2+24].split(b'\x00')[0].decode()
        if segname == '__LINKEDIT':
            new_li_vmsize = (len(output) - new_li_fileoff + 0xFFF) & ~0xFFF
            struct.pack_into('<Q', output, off2+24, new_li_vmaddr)
            struct.pack_into('<Q', output, off2+32, new_li_vmsize)
            struct.pack_into('<Q', output, off2+40, new_li_fileoff)
            struct.pack_into('<Q', output, off2+48, len(output) - new_li_fileoff)
            print(f"__LINKEDIT: vm=0x{new_li_vmaddr:x}+0x{new_li_vmsize:x} file=0x{new_li_fileoff:x}+0x{len(output)-new_li_fileoff:x}")
    elif cmd == 0x02:  # LC_SYMTAB
        old_symoff = struct.unpack_from('<I', output, off2+8)[0]
        old_stroff = struct.unpack_from('<I', output, off2+16)[0]
        if old_symoff > 0:
            struct.pack_into('<I', output, off2+8, old_symoff + li_shift)
        if old_stroff > 0:
            struct.pack_into('<I', output, off2+16, old_stroff + li_shift)
        print(f"LC_SYMTAB: symoff 0x{old_symoff:x}->0x{old_symoff+li_shift:x}")
    elif cmd == 0x26:  # LC_FUNCTION_STARTS
        old = struct.unpack_from('<I', output, off2+8)[0]
        if old > 0:
            struct.pack_into('<I', output, off2+8, old + li_shift)
    elif cmd == 0x2a:  # LC_DATA_IN_CODE
        old = struct.unpack_from('<I', output, off2+8)[0]
        if old > 0:
            struct.pack_into('<I', output, off2+8, old + li_shift)
    elif cmd == 0x1d:  # LC_CODE_SIGNATURE
        old = struct.unpack_from('<I', output, off2+8)[0]
        if old > 0:
            struct.pack_into('<I', output, off2+8, old + li_shift)
    off2 += cmdsize

# Update class_ro_t method list pointers
for ptr_off, old_ml in method_list_refs:
    new_vm = ml_ptr_fixups[old_ml]
    struct.pack_into('<Q', output, ptr_off, new_vm)

with open('libFosterPlatform.dylib', 'wb') as f:
    f.write(output)
print(f"\nWrote libFosterPlatform.dylib: {len(output)} bytes")

# Verify
print("\nVerification:")
off2 = 32
ncmds_v = struct.unpack_from('<I', output, 16)[0]
seg_idx = 0
for i in range(ncmds_v):

    if cmd == 0x19:
        segname = output[off2+8:off2+24].split(b'\x00')[0].decode()
        vmaddr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', output, off2+24)[0]
        vmsize = struct.unpack_from('<Q', output, off2+32)[0]
        fileoff = struct.unpack_from('<Q', output, off2+40)[0]
        filesize = struct.unpack_from('<Q', output, off2+48)[0]
        initprot = struct.unpack_from('<I', output, off2+60)[0]
        print(f"  [{seg_idx}] {segname:16s} vm=0x{vmaddr:x}+0x{vmsize:x} file=0x{fileoff:x}+0x{filesize:x} prot={initprot}")
        seg_idx += 1
    elif cmd == 0x80000022:
        vals = struct.unpack_from('<12I', output, off2)
        print(f"  LC_DYLD_INFO_ONLY: rebase=0x{vals[2]:x}+{vals[3]} bind=0x{vals[4]:x}+{vals[5]}")
        # Check first byte of rebase
        fb = output[vals[2]]
        print(f"    Rebase first byte: 0x{fb:02x}")

$ Bash


Swap __MLDATA and __LINKEDIT segment order
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import struct

# Quick fix: swap __MLDATA to be before __LINKEDIT in load commands
# and fix the rebase segment index

with open('libFosterPlatform.dylib', 'rb') as f:
    data = bytearray(f.read())

# Find all segment commands
off = 32
ncmds = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, 16)[0]
sizeofcmds = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, 20)[0]
seg_cmds = []  # (offset, name, cmdsize)

for i in range(ncmds):
    cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack_from('<II', data, off)
    if cmd == 0x19:
        segname = data[off+8:off+24].split(b'\x00')[0].decode()
        seg_cmds.append((off, segname, cmdsize))
    off += cmdsize

print("Current segment order:")
for i, (off, name, sz) in enumerate(seg_cmds):
    print(f"  [{i}] {name} at cmd offset {off}")

# We need __MLDATA before __LINKEDIT
# Currently: __TEXT, __DATA_CONST, __DATA, __LINKEDIT, __MLDATA
# Want: __TEXT, __DATA_CONST, __DATA, __MLDATA, __LINKEDIT

# Find __LINKEDIT and __MLDATA commands
li_idx = next(i for i, (_, n, _) in enumerate(seg_cmds) if n == '__LINKEDIT')
ml_idx = next(i for i, (_, n, _) in enumerate(seg_cmds) if n == '__MLDATA')

li_off, _, li_sz = seg_cmds[li_idx]
ml_off, _, ml_sz = seg_cmds[ml_idx]

# Save both commands
li_cmd = bytes(data[li_off:li_off+li_sz])
ml_cmd = bytes(data[ml_off:ml_off+ml_sz])

# Since __LINKEDIT is at cmd offset li_off and __MLDATA at ml_off,
# and ml_off > li_off (MLDATA comes after LINKEDIT),
# we need to swap them. But they might not be adjacent.
# Actually, they're not even adjacent - there are other load commands between.
# The simplest: write __MLDATA where __LINKEDIT is, and __LINKEDIT where __MLDATA is.
# But they might be different sizes.

# __LINKEDIT: segment_command_64 = 72 bytes (no sections)
# __MLDATA: segment_command_64 = 72 bytes (no sections)
# Same size! So we can swap in place.

assert li_sz == 72 and ml_sz == 72, f"Sizes differ: li={li_sz} ml={ml_sz}"

data[li_off:li_off+72] = ml_cmd
data[ml_off:ml_off+72] = li_cmd

print("\nSwapped __MLDATA and __LINKEDIT positions")

# Now verify and fix rebase segment indices
# After swap: seg 3 = __MLDATA, seg 4 = __LINKEDIT
# The rebase entries for ML used segment 3, which was wrong (was __LINKEDIT)
# Now segment 3 IS __MLDATA, so the rebase entries are correct!

# But wait, I need to verify - the original rebase entries used segments 1 and 2
# and ML entries used 3. After the swap, seg 3 = __MLDATA. That's correct.

# Verify
print("\nVerification:")
off = 32
seg_idx = 0
for i in range(ncmds):
    cmd, cmdsize = struct.unpack_from('<II', data, off)
    if cmd == 0x19:
        segname = data[off+8:off+24].split(b'\x00')[0].decode()
        vmaddr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, off+24)[0]
        vmsize = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, off+32)[0]
        fileoff = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, off+40)[0]
        filesize = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, off+48)[0]
        initprot = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, off+60)[0]
        print(f"  [{seg_idx}] {segname:16s} vm=0x{vmaddr:x}+0x{vmsize:x} file=0x{fileoff:x}+0x{filesize:x} prot={initprot}")
        seg_idx += 1
    off += cmdsize

with open('libFosterPlatform.dylib', 'wb') as f:
    f.write(data)
print(f"\nWrote {len(data)} bytes")
PYEOF

$ Bash


Check category and all method lists for unconverted entries
python3 -c "
import struct

with open('libFosterPlatform.dylib','rb') as f:
    data = f.read()

# Check category
catlist_off = 0x1c1b20
catlist_size = 0x8
cat_ptr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, catlist_off)[0]
print(f'Category at 0x{cat_ptr:x}')

if 0 < cat_ptr < len(data):
    # category_t: name(8), cls(8), instanceMethods(8), classMethods(8), protocols(8), instanceProperties(8)
    name_ptr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cat_ptr)[0]
    cls_ptr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cat_ptr + 8)[0]
    inst_methods = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cat_ptr + 16)[0]
    class_methods = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cat_ptr + 24)[0]
    protos = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cat_ptr + 32)[0]
    props = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cat_ptr + 40)[0]
    
    if 0 < name_ptr < len(data):
        name = data[name_ptr:name_ptr+30].split(b'\x00')[0].decode('ascii',errors='replace')
    else:
        name = f'ptr=0x{name_ptr:x}'
    
    print(f'  name: {name}')
    print(f'  cls: 0x{cls_ptr:x}')
    print(f'  instanceMethods: 0x{inst_methods:x}')
    print(f'  classMethods: 0x{class_methods:x}')
    
    # Check if method lists are in __objc_methlist and have relative flag
    methlist_off = 0x182820
    methlist_end = methlist_off + 0xd04
    
    for ml_name, ml_addr in [('instanceMethods', inst_methods), ('classMethods', class_methods)]:
        if ml_addr == 0: continue
        if methlist_off <= ml_addr < methlist_end:
            flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_addr)[0]
            count = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_addr + 4)[0]
            is_small = flags & 0x80000000
            print(f'  {ml_name}: addr=0x{ml_addr:x} flags=0x{flags:x} count={count} {\"SMALL!\" if is_small else \"absolute\"}')
        else:
            # Check if it's in our new __MLDATA
            new_ml_vmaddr = 0x1d4000
            if ml_addr >= new_ml_vmaddr:
                ml_fileoff = 0x1d0000 + (ml_addr - new_ml_vmaddr)
                if ml_fileoff < len(data):
                    flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_fileoff)[0]
                    count = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_fileoff + 4)[0]
                    is_small = flags & 0x80000000
                    print(f'  {ml_name}: vmaddr=0x{ml_addr:x} flags=0x{flags:x} count={count} {\"SMALL!\" if is_small else \"absolute\"}')
                else:
                    print(f'  {ml_name}: vmaddr=0x{ml_addr:x} OUTSIDE FILE')
            else:
                print(f'  {ml_name}: addr=0x{ml_addr:x} (unknown location)')

# Check ALL method list pointers in class_ro_t structures
print('\\n=== All class method lists ===')
classlist_off = 0x1c1a98
for i in range(0x88 // 8):
    class_ptr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, classlist_off + i * 8)[0]
    if not (0 < class_ptr < len(data)): continue
    for label in ['class', 'meta']:
        cur = class_ptr
        if label == 'meta':
            cur = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, class_ptr)[0]
            if not (0 < cur < len(data)): break
        ro = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, cur + 32)[0]
        if not (0 < ro < len(data)): continue
        ml = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, ro + 32)[0]
        if ml == 0: continue
        
        name_ptr = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, ro + 24)[0]
        name = data[name_ptr:name_ptr+25].split(b'\x00')[0].decode('ascii',errors='replace') if 0 < name_ptr < len(data) else '?'
        
        # Determine location
        if 0x182820 <= ml < 0x182820 + 0xd04:
            flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml)[0]
            status = 'STILL RELATIVE!' if flags & 0x80000000 else 'in __TEXT (absolute)'
        elif ml >= 0x1d4000:
            ml_fo = 0x1d0000 + (ml - 0x1d4000)
            if ml_fo < len(data):
                flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_fo)[0]
                status = 'STILL RELATIVE!' if flags & 0x80000000 else f'in __MLDATA'
            else:
                status = 'OUT OF FILE'
        else:
            status = f'unknown loc 0x{ml:x}'
        
        print(f'  {name:30s} {label:5s} ml=0x{ml:x} {status}')
"

Search for remaining un-decoded chained fixup entries
python3 -c "
import struct

with open('libFosterPlatform.dylib','rb') as f:
    data = f.read()

# Search DATA segments for values that look like chained fixup entries
# Chained fixup: has non-zero bits in positions 36-62 that form high8/reserved/next fields
# Valid rebased pointers for this binary should be < 0x200000 (vmsize ~ 0x1d4000)

suspicious = []
for seg_name, start, end in [
    ('__DATA_CONST', 0x1bc000, 0x1c4000),
    ('__DATA', 0x1c4000, 0x1d0000),
]:
    for off in range(start, min(end, len(data)), 8):
        val = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, off)[0]
        if val == 0: continue
        # Check if value has bits above 35 that don't look like a valid pointer
        # Valid pointers: < 0x200000 (vmaddr space of this dylib)
        # or 0 (bind target)
        # or > 0x7FFF00000000 (system library addresses, but these shouldn't be in file)
        if val > 0x200000 and val < 0x7FFF00000000:
            # Could be a legitimate constant (float, int, etc.)
            # But chained fixup entries have specific structure
            bind_bit = (val >> 63) & 1
            next_field = ((val >> 51) & 0xFFF)
            # If next_field is non-zero or the value is in the range of typical fixup entries
            if next_field > 0 and next_field < 0x1000:
                # Also check: for a rebase, target (bits 0-35) should be < vmsize
                target = val & 0xFFFFFFFFF
                if target < 0x200000:
                    suspicious.append((off, val, seg_name))

print(f'Found {len(suspicious)} suspicious values')
for off, val, seg in suspicious[:10]:
    # What section?
    sections = {
        '__got': (0x1bc000, 0x1bcda8),
        '__const_dc': (0x1bcdb0, 0x1c0858),
        '__cfstring': (0x1c0858, 0x1c1a98),
        '__objc_const': (0x1c4000, 0x1c6ff0),
        '__objc_selrefs': (0x1c6ff0, 0x1c8498),
        '__objc_classrefs': (0x1c8498, 0x1c86b0),
        '__objc_superrefs': (0x1c86b0, 0x1c86f8),
        '__objc_data': (0x1c89b8, 0x1c8f08),
        '__data': (0x1c8fb0, 0x1ce108),
    }
    sect = 'unknown'
    for sn, (ss, se) in sections.items():
        if ss <= off < se:
            sect = sn
            break
    bind = (val >> 63) & 1
    next_v = ((val >> 51) & 0xFFF) * 4
    target = val & 0xFFFFFFFFF
    print(f'  0x{off:x} ({sect}): 0x{val:016x} bind={bind} next={next_v} target=0x{target:x}')
"

import struct

with open('libFosterPlatform.dylib','rb') as f:
    data = f.read()

# SDLApplication class method list at vmaddr 0x1d4238
# In file: 0x1d0000 + (0x1d4238 - 0x1d4000) = 0x1d0238
ml_foff = 0x1d0238
flags = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_foff)[0]
count = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_foff + 4)[0]
print(f'SDLApplication class ML: flags=0x{flags:x} count={count}')

for j in range(count):
    eoff = ml_foff + 8 + j * 24
    name = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, eoff)[0]
    types = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, eoff + 8)[0]
    imp = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, eoff + 16)[0]
    
    if 0 < name < len(data):
        s = data[name:name+40].split(b'\x00')[0].decode('ascii',errors='replace')
        print(f'  [{j}] name=0x{name:x}(\"{s}\") types=0x{types:x} imp=0x{imp:x}')
    else:
        print(f'  [{j}] name=0x{name:x} types=0x{types:x} imp=0x{imp:x}')

# Also check: Cocoa_WindowListener (most methods, likely to have issues)
# ML at vmaddr 0x1d4d80 -> file offset 0x1d0d80
ml_foff2 = 0x1d0d80
flags2 = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_foff2)[0]
count2 = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_foff2 + 4)[0]
print(f'\\nCocoa_WindowListener ML: flags=0x{flags2:x} count={count2}')
for j in range(min(count2, 5)):
    eoff = ml_foff2 + 8 + j * 24
    name = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, eoff)[0]
    types = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, eoff + 8)[0]
    imp = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, eoff + 16)[0]
    if 0 < name < len(data):
        s = data[name:name+40].split(b'\x00')[0].decode('ascii',errors='replace')
        print(f'  [{j}] name=0x{name:x}(\"{s}\") types=0x{types:x} imp=0x{imp:x}')
    else:
        print(f'  [{j}] name=0x{name:x} types=0x{types:x} imp=0x{imp:x}')

# Check a specific concern: are method IMP pointers reasonable?
# IMPs should be in __text section (0x9de0 to 0x181fe6)
print(f'\\n=== Checking IMP ranges (should be in 0x9de0..0x181fe6) ===')
total_bad_imp = 0
for class_name, ml_vm in [('SDL_RumbleMotor', 0x1d4000), ('SDLApplication', 0x1d4238), 
                           ('Cocoa_WindowListener', 0x1d4d80)]:
    ml_fo = 0x1d0000 + (ml_vm - 0x1d4000)
    cnt = struct.unpack_from('<I', data, ml_fo + 4)[0]
    for j in range(cnt):
        eoff = ml_fo + 8 + j * 24
        imp = struct.unpack_from('<Q', data, eoff + 16)[0]
        if imp < 0x9de0 or imp > 0x1bc000:
            print(f'  {class_name}[{j}]: BAD IMP 0x{imp:x}')
            total_bad_imp += 1
print(f'Total bad IMPs: {total_bad_imp}')
"
